### [1] [Formalizing Latent Thoughts: Four Axioms of Thought Representation in LLMs](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.27378)
*Fahd Seddik,Fatemeh Fard*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: 本文提出了一套基于四条功能公理（因果性、最小性、可分离性、稳定性）的评估框架，用于衡量LLM中的潜在思维表征质量。通过对23个推理任务的审计发现，没有任何模型能同时满足所有四条公理，且表征在区分同一任务内不同问题时存在缺陷，该问题在各类模型家族中普遍存在。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有评估方法将表征质量与模型能力混为一谈，导致无法区分失败是源于表征本身还是处理表征的模型。因此需要一种独立于下游基准分数的、直接衡量表征质量的评估框架。

Method: 形式化定义了四条功能公理（Causality, Minimality, Separability, Stability），并为每条公理设计了直接作用于表征的定量度量，不依赖下游任务准确率。对23个推理任务上的开源权重LLM进行了审计。

Result: 1) 没有任何候选模型能同时满足所有四条公理；2) 表征能可靠区分任务类型，但无法区分同一任务内的不同问题；3) 表征编码的信息量很少超出输入嵌入本身。该失败在密集模型、推理蒸馏模型和RL训练模型中一致性存在。

Conclusion: 当前LLM中的潜在思维表征存在结构性缺陷，而非规模或训练方法的差异所致，表明表征质量问题是更深层的架构性问题。

Abstract: We introduce an axiomatic evaluation framework for latent thought representations in LLMs, comprising metrics that are independent of downstream benchmark scores and reveal representational failures that benchmark accuracy masks. Existing evaluations conflate representation quality with model capacity. Therefore, failures cannot be attributed to the representation rather than to the model that processes it. We formalize four functional axioms (Causality, Minimality, Separability, and Stability) and define a quantitative measure for each, computed directly on the representation independently of downstream accuracy. We audit open-weight LLMs across 23 reasoning tasks (e.g., Spatial Reasoning, Factual QA). We find that no candidate satisfies all four axioms simultaneously, that the representations distinguish task type reliably but cannot distinguish between two questions within the same task, and that the representations encode little information beyond what is already present in the input embedding. The failure is consistent across dense, reasoning-distilled, and RL-trained model families, indicating that the gap is structural rather than a property of model size or training procedure.

</details>


### [2] [Position: The Term "Machine Unlearning" Is Overused in LLMs](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.27379)
*Sangyeon Yoon,Yeachan Jun,Albert No*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: 本文指出LLM研究中"机器遗忘"一词被过度泛化，主张应严格限定为数据集级别的删除（即模型行为与重新训练无差异），并呼吁区分不同类型任务（如对齐、抑制、编辑等），要求术语、基准和评估方法应与实际目标匹配。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 当前LLM领域将"遗忘"标签泛用于多种不同的任务（如拒绝有害请求、实体/知识删除等），导致术语混淆、基准误用、评估失真，论文希望澄清这一概念混乱。

Method: 通过立场论述，提出术语使用的严格界定，区分"遗忘"与对齐、抑制、编辑、混淆等不同任务，并分析当前混淆带来的具体问题（如评估指标误用、隐含保证不匹配）。

Result: 指出现有"遗忘"研究存在表面层次的信息隐藏（如低ROUGE/遗忘准确率）被奖励，而真正的重训练等价性并未验证，派生能力保持被忽视。

Conclusion: 呼吁建立更严格的术语体系，要求术语与显式保证和参考模型挂钩，评估方法需匹配声称的目标。

Abstract: Large language models increasingly face demands to "forget" training data, knowledge, or behaviors due to regulatory deletion obligations, copyright/licensing disputes, and safety or product-policy requirements. This position paper argues that machine unlearning is overused as a term in LLM research and should be reserved for dataset-defined deletion: removing the training influence of a precisely specified forget set such that the resulting model is approximately indistinguishable from retraining without that data. We contend that many tasks currently labeled "unlearning" (e.g., refusal for harmful requests, entity/knowledge removal, or targeted suppression) pursue different, often policy-dependent objectives and therefore require different terminology and baselines (e.g., alignment, suppression, editing, obfuscation). We further argue that this confusion is not cosmetic: because papers make different implicit guarantees under the same label, metrics and benchmarks are frequently reused outside their intended scope, rewarding surface-level non-disclosure (e.g., low ROUGE/forget accuracy) even when retraining-equivalence is not tested and derived capabilities remain. We conclude by calling for stricter terminology tied to explicit guarantees and reference models, and for evaluations that match the claimed objective.

</details>


### [3] [Cognitive Episodes in LLM Reasoning Traces Enable Interpretable Human Item Difficulty Prediction](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.28186)
*Chenguang Wang,Ming Li,Xinyue Zeng,Zhuochun Li,Hong Jiao,Tianyi Zhou,Dawei Zhou*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: 本文提出Epi2Diff框架，将大推理模型的推理轨迹映射为认知驱动的片段序列，通过推理规模、努力分配和状态转换等片段动态特征来建模人类题目难度，在四个真实数据集上优于现有方法，并在SAT分类基准上取得8.1%的平均相对提升。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有题目难度预测方法依赖昂贵的人工校准或文本表示，缺乏对解题认知过程的可解释证据。作者认为难度不仅是文本属性，更是解题负担的可观测结果，因此需要一种可扩展、可解释的基于推理过程证据的建模方法。

Method: 提出Epi2Diff框架，将大推理模型(LRM)的推理轨迹划分为多个认知片段（episodes），每个片段对应一个功能性问题求解状态；提取紧凑的片段动态特征（如推理规模、努力分配、状态转换模式），并与语义表示结合用于人类难度预测。

Result: 在四个真实人类难度数据集上优于微调小模型、LLM上下文学习和监督微调等基线方法；在SAT分类基准上相比监督微调基线获得8.1%平均相对提升；分析表明更难题目引发更费力、迭代性和以实施为中心的片段动态，而非仅更长回答。

Conclusion: LRM推理轨迹中的认知片段为人类题目难度提供了可预测且可解释的过程表示，为教育测量领域提供了结合推理模型的新视角。

Abstract: Predicting human item difficulty is central to educational assessment, where reliable estimates support fairness and effective test construction. Existing methods often depend on costly human calibration or item-level textual representations, providing limited evidence about the cognitive processes that make items difficult. We argue that difficulty should be viewed not only as a property of item text, but also as an observable consequence of the problem-solving burden an item induces. Large Reasoning Models (LRMs) offer scalable process evidence through reasoning traces, but such evidence must be structured to support interpretable modeling. To this end, we introduce Epi2Diff (Episode to Difficulty), a framework that maps LRM reasoning traces into cognitively grounded episode sequences. These episodes group trace segments into functional problem-solving states, enabling difficulty to be modeled through reasoning scale, effort allocation, and state transitions. Epi2Diff extracts compact episode-dynamic features and combines them with semantic item representations for human difficulty prediction. Experiments on four real-world human difficulty datasets show that Epi2Diff consistently outperforms strong baselines, including fine-tuned small language models, LLM in-context learning, and supervised LLM adaptation. On SAT-derived classification benchmarks, Epi2Diff achieves an 8.1% average relative gain over supervised LLM fine-tuning baselines. Further analyses show that harder items induce more effortful, iterative, and implementation-centered episode dynamics, rather than merely longer responses. These results demonstrate that cognitive episodes in LRM reasoning traces provide a predictive and interpretable process representation for human item difficulty, offering a new lens for educational measurement with reasoning models.

</details>


### [4] [A Survey of Automated Presentation Coaching: Systems, Methods, and Open Challenges](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.27380)
*Wen Liang,Li Siyan,Zackary Rackauckas,Julia Hirschberg*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: 本文系统综述了自动化演讲辅导系统，从发音、韵律、流畅度和内容忠实度等维度对现有系统进行分类和评估，并指出了技术挑战和研究空白。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 尽管自动化口述演讲辅导涉及CAPT、韵律建模和语音合成等多个交叉领域，但此前缺乏对这些系统的系统性综述和比较，作者试图填补这一空白。

Method: 提出五维任务分类法（音段发音、词重音、超音段韵律、节奏、内容忠实度），将现有系统映射到该分类体系以揭示覆盖缺口，并梳理其核心技术方法（TTS示例生成与诊断方法）。

Result: 明确了现有系统在各维度上的覆盖情况，指出了标注演讲语料稀缺、跨口音公平反馈、低延迟实时诊断等关键挑战。

Conclusion: 自动化演讲辅导系统在多个维度上仍存在覆盖缺口，未来研究需重点解决数据稀缺、口音公平性和实时性等问题。

Abstract: Automated coaching for oral presentations sits at the intersection of computer-assisted pronunciation training (CAPT), prosody modeling, and speech synthesis, yet no prior work has systematically surveyed and compared existing systems along these dimensions. This survey reviews and categorizes automated presentation coaching systems, spanning pronunciation tutors, fluency and prosody coaches, multimodal trainers, and conference Q&A practice tools. We introduce a five-dimensional task taxonomy - covering segmental pronunciation, lexical stress, suprasegmental prosody, pacing, and content faithfulness - and explicitly map surveyed systems onto it to reveal coverage gaps. We further review the core technical methods these systems employ: TTS-based exemplar generation and diagnostic methods for pronunciation, prosody, and fluency assessment. Key open challenges include the scarcity of annotated presentation corpora, achieving accent-fair feedback across diverse L1 backgrounds, and delivering low-latency diagnostics for real-time rehearsal.

</details>


### [5] [Causal Connections: Leveraging Multilingual Fine-Tuning for Financial QA@FinCausal 2026](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.27446)
*Akash Kumar Gautam,Serhii Hamotskyi,Christian Hänig*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: 本文介绍了团队HSA_CORAL在FinCausal 2026共享任务中的提交，通过抽取式问答从金融叙述中提取因果关系。比较了三种模型家族：编码器-only的标记标注（多语言BERT）、编码器-解码器生成（多语言BART）和解码器-only的LLM（Llama 3.1和GPT变体）。最佳系统是基于GPT-4.1 Mini在英西双语训练数据上微调，在英语子任务中获得并列最高分（4.8140），西班牙语子任务中排名第三（4.7753）。结果表明任务特定适应和多语言微调对于跨语言迁移在金融因果QA中的价值。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 从金融叙事文本中自动提取因果关系对金融分析至关重要，但现有方法在跨语言场景下表现有限，亟需探索不同建模范式在英西双语金融因果抽取任务中的效果。

Method: 比较三种建模家族：(i) 编码器-only的标记标注（多语言BERT）；(ii) 编码器-解码器生成（多语言BART）；(iii) 解码器-only的LLM（Llama 3.1和GPT变体），采用提示优化、少样本示例和 supervised fine-tuning。最终最佳系统为在英西双语训练数据上微调的GPT-4.1 Mini。

Result: 最佳系统GPT-4.1 Mini在英语子任务中获得并列最高分4.8140，西班牙语子任务中排名第三，得分4.7753。少样本和提示方法表现有竞争力，但 supervised fine-tuning 带来的提升最大。

Conclusion: 任务特定适应和多语言微调对于金融因果关系问答中的跨语言迁移非常有效，双语训练数据上的微调能同时提升英语和西班牙语的表现。

Abstract: This paper describes team HSA_CORAL's submission to the FinCausal 2026 shared task on extracting cause-effect relations from financial narratives via extractive question answering in English and Spanish. We compare three modeling families: (i) encoder-only token tagging with multilingual BERT, (ii) encoder-decoder generation with multilingual BART, and (iii) decoder-only LLMs (Llama 3.1 and GPT variants) using prompt refinement, few-shot demonstrations, and supervised fine-tuning. Across settings, prompting and few-shot examples yield competitive performance, while supervised fine-tuning provides the largest gains. Our best system, GPT-4.1 Mini fine-tuned on combined English and Spanish training data, achieves a tied highest score on the English subtask (score 4.8140) and ranks third on Spanish (score 4.7753) under the shared task's LLM-as-a-judge metric. Overall, the results highlight the value of task-specific adaptation and multilingual fine-tuning for cross-lingual transfer in financial causality QA.

</details>


### [6] [Developmental approach reveals the statistical learning of Neural Language Models: Transformers generalize from the most abstract statistical patterns](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.27460)
*Wang Bojun,Holly Jenkins,Elizabeth Wonnacott*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: 本研究通过训练生成式Transformer模型并分析其学习路径，发现神经语言模型先习得抽象全局统计知识，后习得局部统计依赖，早期存在过度泛化现象，后期逐渐收敛。基于此提出了新的统计学习与语言认知框架。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 探究神经语言模型（NLM）在训练过程中的统计学习机制和内部表征变化，理解其语言认知的底层逻辑。

Method: 采用发展性方法，在合成语法上训练一系列生成式Transformer模型，在训练多个阶段保存模型状态，分析内部表征的变化轨迹。

Result: NLMs学习路径呈现"先全局后局部"模式：早期习得最抽象的全局统计知识，后期习得相对局部的统计依赖；早期存在大量过度泛化，后期逐渐受到约束。

Conclusion: 基于观察结果，提出了一个解释NLM统计学习与语言认知的新框架。

Abstract: In this study, we use a developmental approach to investigate the statistical learning and mental representation of neural language models (NLM). A series of Generative Transformer models are trained on a synthetic grammar. The model states are saved at multiple stages in the course of training. Through analyzing how the internal representations of these models change in the developmental path, we found that NLMs acquire the most abstract global statistical knowledge at the beginning of learning and later acquire the relatively local statistical dependencies. This learning path contains many over-generalizations from the very beginning and these over-generalizations are gradually constrained in the later stage of learning. Based on this observation, we propose a new framework to explain the statistical learning and language cognition of NLMs.

</details>


### [7] [Supersede: Diagnosing and Training the Memory-Update Gap in LLM Agents](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.27472)
*Vedant Patel*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: 本文发现LLM智能体在长对话中无法正确追踪事实变化（事实废弃问题），即使使用GPT-5.4这类前沿模型，从完整上下文切换到自维护记忆时准确率从92%骤降至77%。问题根源是记忆维护而非理解能力，且随对话长度增加而恶化。作者发布了Supersede环境，并通过GRPO微调小模型（Qwen2.5-3B）将准确率从9.0%提升至16.7%，首次证明该差距可通过训练弥补。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有LLM智能体在长对话中无法正确处理事实更新（如用户搬家、价格变动），系统性地使用过时信息。作者希望隔离并量化这一"事实废弃"问题，并探索是否可以通过训练解决。

Method: 1) 在LongMemEval的知识更新子集上进行基准测试，对比全上下文vs自维护记忆。2) 分析记忆大小和对话长度的影响。3) 构建Supersede强化学习环境（基于verifiers/prime-rl），奖励回答当前事实、惩罚过时事实。4) 使用GRPO对Qwen2.5-3B进行微调。

Result: 1) 前沿模型(gpt-5.4)从全上下文（92%）切换到自维护记忆（77%）显著下降。2) 对话长度增长24倍，准确率从68%降至28%，增加记忆大小无改善。3) GRPO微调使Qwen2.5-3B在未见对话上准确率从9.0%提升至16.7%。

Conclusion: 事实废弃问题是LLM智能体的根本性瓶颈，根源在记忆维护而非理解能力，且不能仅靠更大模型或更大记忆解决。但该问题可通过强化学习训练来缓解，这是首个证据表明该差距是可训练的。

Abstract: Large language model (LLM) agents operate over long, multi-session interactions in which facts change: a user moves, a price updates, a plan is revised. Acting correctly requires using the current value of a fact and discarding values that have been superseded. We isolate this ability on real conversational data and show that it is a distinct, unsolved failure. On the knowledge-update subset of LongMemEval, replacing an agent's full context with a bounded, self-maintained memory drops accuracy from 92% to 77% even on a frontier model (gpt-5.4), a gap that is statistically significant (paired McNemar p<0.005) and persists across model scale while full-context accuracy saturates near 92%. The bottleneck is therefore memory maintenance, not comprehension, and is not closed by a stronger model. We then ask whether this is merely an undersized memory, and find it is not: as the conversation grows 24x, accuracy falls further (from 68% to 28%), and granting the agent proportionally more memory yields no detectable recovery (28% to 28%, n=25). The failure scales with the length of the conversation, not the compression ratio. We release Supersede, an open reinforcement-learning environment (on the verifiers / prime-rl stack) that turns this measurement into a training signal: agents are rewarded for answering from the current value and penalized for stale ones. Finally, we close the loop and show the gap is trainable: GRPO fine-tuning a small open model (Qwen2.5-3B) on this environment nearly doubles its held-out supersession accuracy on real, unseen conversations (9.0% to 16.7%, a single run), along a monotonic checkpoint curve indicating the learned policy, not the harness, carries the gain. To our knowledge this is the first trainable environment whose reward targets temporal fact-currency, and the first evidence the supersession gap can be trained down, not only measured.

</details>


### [8] [The Context-Ready Transformer](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.27538)
*Mahesh Godavarti*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: 本文提出Context-Ready Transformer，一种通过D层Transformer模块前增加预上下文化机制的新型循环神经网络架构。在从左到右生成时，校正网络将上一位置的块输出（缓存的过去上下文摘要）与当前token嵌入结合，使token进入模块时已被上下文化。推理时形成循环神经网络；训练时将校正过程展开K次并行处理。预训练Transformer可转换为该模型。实验表明D=5模型超越12层Transformer且速度快1.7倍；D=1模型（K=10）超越6层Transformer且速度快2.6倍。该架构受益于宽表示和长上下文，在指针追踪任务上D=1模型解决全部10个组合层级。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 解决标准Transformer在自回归生成时无法高效利用已生成的上下文信息，每个token以原始嵌入进入Transformer模块缺乏上下文感知的问题。同时希望在保持并行训练效率的同时，获得循环神经网络在序列推理上的优势。

Method: 提出一种结合Transformer与循环神经网络的新架构：1）在D层Transformer块前增加预上下文化机制；2）设计校正网络（correction network），将上一位置的块输出与当前token嵌入结合；3）训练时展开校正过程K次，实现全序列并行处理；4）支持从预训练Transformer通过添加零初始化的校正FFN和微调进行转换。

Result: D=5模型超越12层Transformer，推理速度快1.7倍（A100上）；D=1模型（K=10）超越6层Transformer，推理速度快2.6倍；顺序推理与并行K=10的PPL差异不超过0.01；在指针追踪任务上，D=1模型（BPTT训练）解决所有10个组合层级，而标准Transformer呈现阶梯状的深度依赖性。

Conclusion: Context-Ready Transformer在保持并行训练效率的同时，实现了比标准Transformer更高的推理速度和更好的性能，尤其受益于宽表示和长上下文。该架构成功融合了Transformer的并行训练优势与RNN的序列推理优势。

Abstract: We introduce the context-ready transformer, a new recurrent neural network architecture built from a D-layer transformer block that pre-contextualizes each token before it enters the block. During left-to-right generation, a correction network combines the previous position's block output -- a cached summary of past context -- with the current token embedding, so the tokenenters the block already contextualized rather than as a raw embedding. At sequential inference, the correction chain makes the architecture a recurrent neural network. For training, we unroll the correction process K times over the full sequence, processing all positions in parallel at each step. A pretrained transformer can also be converted to a context-ready model by adding a zero-initialized correction FFN and fine-tuning. We evaluate across widths, depths, block sizes, and two datasets, with all comparisons against standard transformers, variants, and ablations. A D=5 model beats a 12-layer transformer while generating 1.7x faster on an A100. With K=10, a single-layermodel (D=1) beats a 6-layer transformer with a 2.6x inference speedup, and sequential inference matches parallel K=10 to within 0.01 PPL. The architecture benefits most from wide representations and long contexts. On a pointer-chasing task, D=1 trained with BPTT solves all 10 composition levels, while standard transformers exhibit staircase-like depth dependence.

</details>


### [9] [EntMTP: Accelerating LLM Inference with Entropy Guided Multi Token Prediction](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.27550)
*Carrie Chen*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: 提出EntMTP，一种无需训练的调度器，根据局部生成熵动态切换树注意力拓扑，使推测深度匹配上下文可预测性，在不牺牲质量下提升多token预测的推理速度，相较于Hydra和Medusa分别获得1.15x和1.36x的加速。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有MTP模型使用静态树注意力拓扑，推测深度在整个生成过程中固定不变，与自然语言的熵模式不一致——低熵区域可支持多步推测，高熵区域需要保守推测，导致计算效率低下。

Method: 提出EntMTP，一个训练免费的调度器，基于局部生成熵的实时估计，从一组任务特定的帕累托最优树中动态切换树注意力拓扑，使推测深度与上下文可预测性相匹配。

Result: 在Humaneval、ShareGPT、GSM8k、Litbench基准上，EntMTP相较于Hydra实现一致1.15x加速，相较于Medusa实现峰值1.36x加速，且不牺牲生成质量。

Conclusion: 通过动态适配推测深度到文本熵模式，EntMTP有效提升了多token预测的推理效率，验证了静态固定拓扑与自然语言分布不匹配的问题。

Abstract: Multi-token prediction has been shown to increase data density during training, improve downstream text-generation quality, and serves as the defacto approach for self-speculative decoding. Existing foundation and open source models that use MTP heads commit to a static tree-based attention topology throughout the entire generation sequence, meaning the speculation depth, and thus the compute required during verification, stays constant regardless of the context. This is fundamentally misaligned with the entropy patterns of natural language where low-entropy regions often support reliable multi-step drafting, while high-entropy regions require more conservative speculation. To address this, we propose Entropy-guided Multi-Token Prediction (EntMTP), a training-free scheduler that toggles between tree-based attention topologies from a set of task-specific pareto-optimal trees conditioned on a running estimate of local generation entropy. By matching speculation depth to context predictability, EntMTP maximizes expected accepted-token throughput across the full distribution of generated text without sacrificing generation quality. When evaluated across Humaneval, ShareGPT, GSM8k, and Litbench benchmarks, EntMTP consistently achieves a 1.15x speedup against Hydra and peak speedup of 1.36x against Medusa baselines respectively.

</details>


### [10] [Ko-WideSearch: A Korean Breadth-Search Benchmark for Exhaustive Set Enumeration by Web Agents](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.27595)
*Minbyul Jeong*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: 本文提出Ko-WideSearch，一个韩语广度搜索基准测试，通过自动合成与验证流程构建，包含228个表格、190个实体和16个类别。实验发现20个Web代理在广度搜索中普遍失败：能恢复集合但无法填充行数据（Item-F1 92.8 vs Row-F1 53.7），且增加搜索量或花费无法弥补差距。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有Web代理基准测试过度聚焦于深度搜索（在一系列约束下找出一个模糊答案），而广度搜索（穷举封闭集合并填充每个条目的属性）几乎未被评估，尤其在非英语环境中。同时，构建广度搜索基准的难度极高——验证黄金集的完整性和每个单元格的正确性远比检查单一答案昂贵。

Method: 提出自动化合成与验证（synthesize-and-verify）流程构建Ko-WideSearch基准。每个任务命名一个集合父实体（如电视剧季、王朝、联赛、行政区、选举），要求列出全部成员并生成每项属性表。通过两个结构旋钮独立调节难度：表格宽度和二维复合键，使交叉乘积成员覆盖率从0%到100%跨越三个难度层级。采用统一的归一化感知比较器用于黄金集构建和评分，避免因格式差异错误丢弃日期和计数列。

Result: 在20个Web代理上，一致性失败模式：代理能恢复集合但无法填充行数据（Item-F1 92.8 vs Row-F1 53.7）；随着难度旋钮加固，准确率稳步下降；增加搜索量或花费无法弥合差距。细粒度分析显示，困难在于找到正确的值而非格式化输出——自由文本单元格最容易失败，而日期或姓名等标准答案单元格通常正确。

Conclusion: 广度搜索是当前Web代理的显著短板，现有方法无法通过增加资源投入解决，需要新的技术突破。自由文本单元格是最具挑战性的部分，提示未来研究应聚焦于信息检索的准确性而非输出格式化。

Abstract: Web-agent benchmarks overwhelmingly measure depth -- pinning one obscure answer behind a chain of constraints -- while breadth, exhaustively enumerating a closed set and filling each item's attributes, is barely evaluated, especially outside English. Breadth is also hard to build: certifying that a gold set is complete and every cell correct is far costlier than checking a single answer. I introduce \textsc{Ko-WideSearch}, a Korean breadth-search benchmark built by an automated synthesize-and-verify pipeline. Each task names a set-parent entity -- a TV season, a dynasty, a league, an administrative region, an election -- and asks for its full membership plus a per-item attribute table, graded by Item-, Column-, and Row-F1. It spans 228 tables over 190 entities and sixteen categories across three difficulty tiers, set by two structural knobs I dial independently -- table width and a 2-D composite key -- so cross-product membership climbs from 0\% to 100\% across the tiers. A single normalization-aware comparator is shared between gold construction and grading, so stable date and count columns are not over-dropped on formatting alone. Across twenty web agents, the failure is consistent: agents recover the set but not the rows (e.g.\ Item-F1 92.8 against Row-F1 53.7), accuracy falls steadily as the knobs harden, and neither more search nor more spend closes the gap. Broken down by cell, the hard part is finding the right value, not formatting it: open-ended free-text cells fail most, while cells with a standard answer such as a date or a name usually come out right.

</details>


### [11] [Narrative-UFET: Narrative Generation for Ultra-Fine Entity Typing](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.27598)
*Mreedul Gupta,Advait Deshmukh,Ashwin Umadi,Matt Pauk,Maria Leonor Pacheco*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: 本文提出 Narrative-UFET，通过自动生成短篇叙事（而非单句）为超细粒度实体类型分类提供上下文，发现叙事上下文（尤其是类型发生变化的变体）能显著提升长尾类型的识别效果，且合成叙事比自然文本更有效。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有UFET方法依赖句子级上下文，但消歧证据常跨句分布，且所有现有资源均为句子级，难以验证多句上下文的实际作用。

Method: 构建Narrative-UFET数据集，为每个实体提及自动生成连贯的短叙事，设计了两种变体：Maintain（实体类型在叙事中保持不变）和Change（类型发生变化）；通过对比句子级基线、自然上下文和合成叙事来评估效果。

Result: 叙事上下文在长尾类型上持续优于句子级基线，Change变体信号更强；合成叙事相比自然上下文带来更大提升。

Conclusion: 合成叙事能揭示自然文本中隐式的消歧信号，表明受控的篇章构造对细粒度实体分类有价值，但仍存在较大改进空间，未来可探索更复杂的篇章建模与叙事生成。

Abstract: Ultra-fine entity typing (UFET) assigns highly specific types to entity mentions, but current approaches struggle with types in the long tail. We hypothesize that a key limitation is the reliance on sentence-level context, since disambiguating evidence is often spread across multiple sentences. Testing this has been difficult because all existing UFET resources are sentence-level. We present Narrative-UFET, a controlled extension of UFET in which each entity mention is paired with an automatically generated short, coherent narrative. Synthesizing narratives lets us isolate the effect of specific discourse properties. We experiment with two paired variants: one in which the entity's type is held constant across the narrative (Maintain) and one in which it shifts (Change). We show that narrative context yields consistent improvements on long-tail types over sentence-level baselines, with the Change variant providing the stronger signal. A comparison against naturally occurring contexts shows that synthetic narratives yield stronger gains, indicating that controlled discourse construction can surface signals that real text leaves implicit. Substantial room for improvement remains, suggesting open directions in both discourse modeling and narrative construction.

</details>


### [12] [Masked Language Flow Models](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.27617)
*Iskander Azangulov,Kianoosh Ashouritaklimi,Leo Zhang,Simon Vary,Patrick Rebeschini*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: 本文提出Masked Language Flow Models (MLFMs)，将掩码机制融入流式语言模型，通过连续随机插值连接部分掩码序列与干净序列，实现快速并行生成与多步推理的兼得，在GSM8K和MT-Bench上首次证明流式语言模型可扩展至下游推理和指令遵循任务。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: Masked Diffusion Models (MDMs)在少步采样时无法有效并行生成，而Flow Language Models (FLMs)虽能单步生成但缺乏多步推理能力。现有方法在快速生成与复杂推理之间存在矛盾。

Method: 提出MLFMs，使用连续随机插值在部分掩码序列与干净序列之间构建连续流，支持条件生成；可将预训练MDMs通过轻量适配转化为MLFMs；设计交替连续去噪与离散置信标记去掩码的新型采样器。

Result: 在GSM8K和MT-Bench上评估，首次证明流式语言模型可扩展至下游推理和指令遵循任务。

Conclusion: MLFMs成功融合了掩码扩散模型的掩码机制与流式语言模型的连续流，在保持并行生成效率的同时提升了多步推理能力，为流式语言模型在复杂任务上的应用开辟了新路径。

Abstract: Masked Diffusion Models (MDMs) promise fast, parallel language generation, but their reverse transition factorises across token positions -- an approximation that breaks down in the few-step sampling regime where parallel generation ought to provide the greatest efficiency gains. Flow Language Models (FLMs) sidestep this limitation by learning a continuous flow that transports noise toward clean sequences represented in Euclidean space, inducing a flow map that can be distilled for single-step generation. However, this makes complex tasks requiring multi-step reasoning problematic for FLMs, as FLMs are forced to decode every token during generation. To address this, we introduce Masked Language Flow Models (MLFMs), which incorporate masking into FLMs using a continuous stochastic interpolant to bridge partially masked and clean sequences. This design enables conditional generation via continuous flows and allows pretrained MDMs to be converted into MLFMs through a simple, lightweight adaptation. Leveraging this flexibility, we propose a novel sampler that alternates continuous denoising with the discrete unmasking of confident tokens to better support multi-step reasoning. We evaluate our approach on GSM8K and MT-Bench and find, for the first time, that flow-based language models can be scaled to solve downstream reasoning and instruction-following tasks.

</details>


### [13] [Cross-Platform Chinese Offensive Comment Detection via Dual-Threshold Hard Example Mining](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.27629)
*Ruixing Ren,Junhui Zhao,Fangfang Wang*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: 针对跨平台部署时性能下降的问题，本文提出了一种双阈值难例挖掘方法。通过微调RoBERTa构建基线，构建多平台测试集，量化域间距离，揭示性能瓶颈；进一步提出双阈值难例挖掘策略，利用预测置信度筛选高、低置信度的易错样本，仅用少量人工标注的难例进行二次微调，实现低成本的跨平台域适应，在四个平台上均取得显著性能提升。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 中文社交媒体攻击性评论检测在跨平台部署时面临严重的性能下降问题，现有方法缺乏对跨平台域迁移瓶颈的系统分析与低成本解决方案。

Method: 首先在COLD数据集上微调RoBERTa作为基线；其次构建覆盖微博、小红书、贴吧、知乎的三分类细粒度测试集，使用Jaccard距离和Proxy-A距离量化域间距离；提出双阈值难例挖掘策略，通过预测置信度从无标注语料中筛选高/低置信度易错样本，仅用少量人工标注的难例进行二次微调。

Result: 优化模型在四个跨平台测试集上均取得了显著的性能提升，验证了双阈值难例挖掘策略在低标注成本下的有效性。

Conclusion: 双阈值难例挖掘是一种低成本、高效的跨平台域适应方法，能够有效缓解中文社交平台攻击性评论检测的跨平台性能退化问题。

Abstract: Cross-platform deployment of offensive comment detection for Chinese social media suffers performance degradation. The paper proposes a dual-threshold hard mining method to address this. First, the clean-Chinese-base RoBERTa is finetuned on COLD to establish a binary baseline for fair comparison. Second, a three-class fine-labeled test set covering Weibo, Xiaohongshu, Tieba, and Zhihu is constructed, domain distances from the source are quantified using Jaccard and Proxy-A Distance, as well as the degradation bottleneck of the baseline under domain shift is systematically revealed. Herein, a dual threshold hard example mining strategy is proposed. High- and low-confidence error-prone samples are filtered from unlabeled corpora by prediction confidence. The model is secondarily finetuned under implicit contexts with merely a small set of manually labeled hard examples, realizing low-cost cross-platform domain adaptation. Experiments reveal significant performance gains of the optimized model across four platforms.

### [14] [Yuvion LLM: An Adversarially-Aware Large Language Model for Content And AI Safety](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.27632)
*Ting Ma,Xiufeng Huang,Benlei Cui,Xiaowen Xu,Shikai Qiu,Ruijie Jian,Hongxing Li,Guanghui Wang,Longtao Huang,Haiwen Hong,Haolei Xu,Wenjing Jiang,Ziwen Xu,Zhaoyu Fan,Shaoxuan He,Chuxi Xiao,Yujian Li,Xinyue Chen,Chunyang Chai,Wenxuan Liu,Ziheng Wang,Dongjie Zhang,Yangfan Zhou,Libin Dong,Yupeng Cao,Xiaoqian Xia,Jing Wang,Zhe Jiang,Zhenan Ye,Guang Yang,Bin Liu,Wei Peng,Ziqiang Zhu,Meihui Lian,Kaiwen Lv Kacuila,Haidong Ding,Bingyu Zhu,Yan Wang,Hai Zhao,Xuan Jin,Wei Zhao,Pengfei Sun,Wei Wang,Huiming Zhang,Bin Li,Hui Xue*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: 本文提出Yuvion LLM，一个将对抗鲁棒性和智能体能力作为首要目标的大语言模型，通过对抗感知数据构建、知识增强继续预训练、策略导向的多任务安全后训练（包括风险感知SFT和强化学习策略优化）以及安全感知的智能体强化学习来提升安全性和对抗鲁棒性。同时引入YLRE基准（93个评测），实验表明Yuvion-8B在多项安全任务上超越包括GPT-5.4和Qwen3-MAX在内的更大模型。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有大语言模型的安全策略忽视了安全问题的对抗性本质，即许多安全失败源于对模型策略和防护的刻意规避，而非自然输入。同时，现有模型在涉及规划、工具使用和多步推理等真实安全场景中表现不足，导致实验室测得的性能高估了实际部署的鲁棒性。

Method: Yuvion LLM的pipeline包括四个关键环节：(1)对抗感知数据构建；(2)知识增强继续预训练；(3)策略导向的多任务安全后训练，包含风险感知监督微调(SFT)和基于强化学习的策略优化；(4)安全感知的智能体强化学习，用于处理涉及工具使用和多步推理的复杂安全场景。

Result: Yuvion LLM在安全评测上表现优异，尤其在对抗条件下展现出强鲁棒性。Yuvion-8B在多项安全任务上超越绝大多数最先进的基线模型，包括GPT-5.4和Qwen3-MAX等参数量显著更大的模型。

Conclusion: 将对抗鲁棒性和智能体能力作为模型开发的"一等公民"目标，可以有效提升大语言模型在真实部署场景中的安全性。Yuvion LLM证明了相对小的模型也能通过针对性的安全设计超越更大的通用模型。

Abstract: As large language models are increasingly deployed in real-world systems, safety failures can still lead to harmful outputs and dangerous misuse. We argue that the essence of safety is adversarial: many failures arise not from natural inputs alone, but from strategic attempts to evade model policies and safeguards. However, existing general-purpose model development largely overlook this adversarial nature, and often remain insufficient for realistic safety scenarios involving planning, tool use, and multi-step reasoning, causing measured safety performance to overestimate real deployment robustness. To address this gap, we present Yuvion LLM, a large language model built for adversarially robust content safety and broader AI safety. Yuvion LLM treats adversarial robustness and agentic capability as first-class objectives. Its pipeline combines adversarially aware data construction, knowledge-enhanced continued pretraining, and policy-grounded multi-task safety post-training, including risk-aware supervised fine-tuning and reinforcement learning-based policy optimization, together with safety-aware agentic reinforcement learning for tool use and multi-step reasoning in complex safety scenarios. We further introduce the Yuvion LLM RiskEval (YLRE), a collection of 93 benchmarks across four evaluation categories, covering diverse open and internal evaluations with a focus on safety, adversarial robustness, and real-world capability requirements. Across these evaluations, Yuvion LLM demonstrates clear advantages on safety-focused benchmarks and particularly strong robustness under adversarial conditions, while maintaining solid overall capability. Notably, Yuvion-8B outperforms most state-of-the-art baselines, including substantially larger models such as GPT-5.4 and Qwen3-MAX, on several safety tasks.

</details>


### [15] [When Search Agents Should Ask: DiscoBench for Clarification-Aware Deep Search](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.27669)
*Yiling Tao,Shihan Deng,Meiling Tao,Pengzhi Wei,Zhichao Hu,Zhihao Zhu*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: 提出了DiscoBench基准，用于评估大语言模型搜索代理在复杂搜索任务中识别模糊性、提出澄清问题和修正推理路径的能力。实验表明，当前搜索代理在模糊检测和有效澄清方面存在显著不足，且反复搜索不如直接猜测。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有基准假设用户查询完整明确，但真实搜索请求常模糊、不明确甚至事实错误，这种模糊性在多步推理中会传播并导致错误搜索轨迹，亟需评估代理的澄清能力。

Method: 构建DiscoBench基准，包含211个样本、463个模糊实例，覆盖11个领域和4种模糊类型；设计用户模拟器实现多轮交互，从任务效用、模糊检测、交互策略、成本效率四个维度评估模型。

Result: 模糊检测和有效澄清是两种独立能力；反复搜索而不主动澄清的表现甚至不如直接猜测；当前搜索代理在检索能力与交互式问题解决之间存在关键差距。

Conclusion: 现有LLM搜索代理在应对模糊查询时存在严重不足，需要更有效的澄清机制来提升深度搜索的可靠性和交互质量。

Abstract: Search agents powered by large language models (LLMs) are increasingly used to solve complex information-seeking tasks, requiring multi-step retrieval and reasoning to fulfill user goals. However, existing benchmarks often assume that user queries are complete and explicit, overlooking the fact that real-world search requests are frequently vague, underspecified, or even factually incorrect. In deep search scenarios, such ambiguity can propagate along multi-step reasoning chains and lead agents toward incorrect search trajectories. To address this gap, we introduce DiscoBench, a benchmark for clarification-aware deep search, designed to evaluate whether search agents can proactively identify ambiguity, ask effective clarification questions, and recover correct reasoning paths through user interaction. DiscoBench contains 211 samples and 463 ambiguity instances across 11 real-world domains, covering four ambiguity types. We further design a user simulator for multi-turn interaction and evaluate model performance from four perspectives: task utility, ambiguity detection, interaction strategy, and cost efficiency. Experiments on representative LLMs show that ambiguity detection and effective clarification are distinct capabilities, and that repeatedly searching instead of asking for clarification often performs worse than direct guessing, highlighting a critical gap between retrieval ability and interactive problem-solving in current search agents.

### [16] [From Signals to Transfer: A Factorised Study of Probe-Based Uncertainty Estimation in Large Language Models](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.27679)
*Ponhvoan Srey,Xiaobao Wu,Cong-Duy Nguyen,Quang Minh Nguyen,Duc Anh Vu,Anh Tuan Luu*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: 本文对基于探针的不确定性估计方法进行了因素分解研究，发现原始隐藏状态和注意力特征在域内表现良好，但在分布偏移下结构化/压缩特征更鲁棒；提示设计和标签构建显著影响探针行为；基于最佳实践训练的预训练探针能较好地迁移到开放式事实生成任务。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有基于探针的不确定性估计方法在特征设计、训练数据构建和评估设置上同时变化，导致无法明确哪些因素真正驱动性能，亟需进行受控条件下的因素分解研究。

Method: 在匹配条件下对探针式UE进行因素分解研究，分别控制特征设计、训练数据构建和评估设置等变量，分析各因素对性能的影响。基于最佳实践训练预训练探针并评估其在开放式事实生成任务上的迁移能力。

Result: 原始隐藏状态和注意力特征在域内难以被超越；分布偏移下结构化/压缩特征更鲁棒；提示设计和标签构建显著影响探针行为；基于基准训练的预训练探针能较好地迁移到开放式事实生成。

Conclusion: 域内性能不足以衡量探针式UE的真实进展，应更多采用面向部署的评估方式，并提供了稳定的基线模型。

Abstract: Probe-based uncertainty estimation (UE) has emerged as a prominent approach to detect hallucinations in Large Language Models (LLMs) by learning uncertainty from internal model signals. Yet, recent methods vary simultaneously across feature design, training data construction, and evaluation setting, obscuring what actually drives performance. To address this issue, we propose a factorised study of probe-based UE under matched conditions. Our results show that raw hidden states and attention features are difficult to outperform in-domain. However, under distribution shift, structured and compressed features are more robust, suggesting that in-domain performance alone is insufficient to measure progress. Furthermore, prompting and label construction significantly affect probe behaviour. Building on these best-practice findings, we train benchmark-based pretrained probes that transfer reasonably well to open-ended factual generation, providing a stable off-the-shelf baseline. Our work encourages more deployment-oriented evaluation of probe-based uncertainty estimators. The code repository is available at https://github.com/ponhvoan/ProbeUE.

</details>

*Maria Thomas,Kristina Gligoric,Nihar B. Shah*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: 本文提出一种通过预注册未来发布的LLM模型来防止p-hacking的研究协议，实验证明该方法能有效阻止大部分p-hack的跨模型迁移。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: LLM用于数据分析时容易被p-hack（通过调整提示词、解码参数等操纵结果），研究者缺乏有效手段防止这种操纵行为。

Method: 研究者先在现有模型上完成实验设计并预注册，同时指定一组未来可用的模型。确认分析在预注册后第一个发布的可选模型上进行，因为该模型在承诺时尚不存在，无法被针对性地hack。

Result: 在20个模型和11种配置下，该协议阻止了73.9%和72.7%的p-hack迁移；预注册实验中有6/7的hack配置在首个未来模型上失效。

Abstract: Large language models (LLMs) are increasingly used to generate, classify, and annotate data whose outputs feed downstream hypothesis tests. However, LLM-based research is easy to p-hack: a researcher can tune the prompts, decoding parameters, or output format until a desired result is reached. We propose a protocol to mitigate p-hacking in LLM-based research: preregistering the experiment and eligible models, and then running it on the first eligible LLM that is released after the preregistration. The researcher finalizes the procedure on current models, preregisters the analysis plan together with a set of eligible future models, and runs the confirmatory analysis on the first eligible model released afterward. Because this model does not exist at commitment time, it cannot be hacked against; furthermore, configurations that hack one model frequently do not transfer to the next. We evaluate the protocol on two tasks whose true values are known. Across 20 models from four providers and 11 LLM-analysis configurations, the protocol would have blocked successful transfer of the p-hack in 73.9% and 72.7% of cases in the two tasks. Additional analyses reveal that mitigation remains substantial under several stress tests. Finally, putting money where our mouth is, we followed our own protocol and preregistered our experiment. The preregistered experiment confirmed the protocol's effectiveness: out of the 7 configurations that hacked the prior model, the hacking failed to carry over in 6 configurations on the first eligible model released afterward.

Across three experiments on four models, our approach reduces jailbreak susceptibility and harmful output rates relative to generic warmth fine-tuning baselines, while preserving conversational warmth. ### [21] [Enhancing Numerical Prediction in LLMs via Smooth MMD Alignment](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.27731)
*Zhuo Zuo,Li Yue,Wenhao Zheng,Chenpeng Wang,Xianggen Liu*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: 本文提出Smooth Maximum Mean Discrepancy (SMMD)损失函数，通过基于数值距离的核和图平滑技术，让大语言模型在数值预测任务上更精确，在数学推理、算术计算、时钟识别和图表问答四个任务上均优于交叉熵等方法。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 标准交叉熵训练将数值token视为无结构类别，忽略了数值之间的距离信息，导致LLM在需要精确数值输出的任务上不可靠。

Method: 提出SMMD，基于MMD引入数值距离核和图平滑：1) 在数值子词表上定义含值距离的核函数；2) 通过核匹配对齐预测分布与目标分布；3) 在核诱导的图上平滑预测-目标残差以促进局部一致性。

Result: 在数学推理、算术计算、时钟识别、图表问答四个数值任务上，SMMD在不同LLM和VLM主干网络上均持续优于交叉熵及其他针对数值的损失函数。

Conclusion: MMD与图平滑之间存在互补效应，基于距离的核设计至关重要；SMMD能有效提升LLM的数值预测精度。

Abstract: Despite their strong general capabilities, large language models (LLMs) often remain unreliable when outputs must be numerically precise. A key reason is the training objective: standard cross-entropy treats numeric tokens as unstructured categories and ignores the metric structure of their values. We address this mismatch with Smooth Maximum Mean Discrepancy (SMMD), which builds on the classic MMD by incorporating value-distance kernels over numeric tokens and graph-based smoothness. With this kernel defined over a numeric sub-vocabulary, SMMD aligns the predicted numeric distribution to the target via kernel matching and smooths the prediction-target residual over the induced kernel graph to encourage local consistency. We evaluate SMMD on four numeric-target tasks: mathematical reasoning, arithmetic calculation, clock-time recognition, and chart question answering, across multiple open-weight LLM and VLM backbones. SMMD consistently improves accuracy over both cross-entropy and recent numeric-target losses; analyses show complementary effects between MMD and smoothness and underscore the importance of distance-based kernel design. Code is available at https://github.com/Zuozhuo/smmd-loss.

### [23] [Output-Space Allocation Costs for Calibration-Guided LLM Compression: An Empirical Study](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.27785)
*Qiong Tang,Xiangkun Hu,Xiangyang Liu,Yiran Chen,Yunfan Shao*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: 本文研究ROCKET压缩方法中分配成本函数的选择问题，发现将权重空间Frobenius误差替换为输出空间目标（ROCKET-ActCost）在Qwen3-8B上50%压缩率时准确率提升0.8个百分点，但困惑度增加16%，且两种成本函数高度相关（>0.99）限制了效果差异，在低压缩率下影响更小。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 当前无训练压缩方法（如ROCKET）在MCKP分配阶段使用权重空间Frobenius误差作为成本，而逐层分解是基于输出重构目标，这种目标不一致可能导致压缩后模型保真度下降。作者旨在探究将分配成本与输出空间目标对齐是否能提升压缩效果。

Method: 将ROCKET中MCKP分配阶段的成本函数从权重空间Frobenius误差替换为输出空间误差（ActCost），在Qwen3-8B（50%压缩率）和Llama-3.2-1B（20%压缩率）上对比两种方法的准确率和困惑度。

Result: Qwen3-8B上50%压缩时：ROCKET-ActCost准确率53.1% vs ROCKET 52.3%（+0.8pp），但困惑度61.46 vs 52.98（+16%）。Llama-3.2-1B上20%压缩时：两者几乎一致（53.3% vs 53.5%准确率，14.45 vs 14.66 PPL）。权重空间与输出空间误差高度相关（>0.99）。

Conclusion: 分配成本函数的选择会导致准确率与困惑度之间的权衡（accuracy-perplexity tradeoff），不同分配目标偏好不同的下游指标；两种成本函数高度相关限制了分配差异，导致效果改善有限；在低压缩率下成本函数的影响更为微小。

Abstract: Training-free compression methods for large language models (LLMs) often use calibration data to guide compression decisions. ROCKET, a recent method combining sparse-dictionary factorization with multi-choice knapsack problem (MCKP) allocation, derives its per-layer factorization from an output reconstruction objective but uses weight-space Frobenius error as the MCKP allocation cost. We investigate whether aligning the allocation cost with the output-space objective improves compressed model fidelity. On Qwen3-8B at 50\% compression, our ROCKET-ActCost achieves +0.8 percentage points higher average accuracy across 8 zero-shot benchmarks (53.1\% vs 52.3\%), but increases WikiText perplexity by 16\% (61.46 vs 52.98). This accuracy-perplexity tradeoff reveals that different allocation objectives favor different downstream metrics. The high correlation ($>$0.99) between weight-space and output-space errors limits allocation divergence, explaining the modest effect size. On Llama-3.2-1B at 20\% compression, the two methods produce near-identical results (53.3\% vs 53.5\% accuracy, 14.45 vs 14.66 PPL), suggesting that the effect of the cost function is minor at lower compression ratios.

### [24] [SHIFT: Gate-Modulated Activation Steering for Knowledge Conflict Mitigation in Retrieval-Augmented Generation](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.27786)
*Ruochang Li,Pengcheng Huang,Zhenghao Liu,Yukun Yan,Huiyuan Xie,Yu Gu,Ge Yu,Maosong Sun*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: 本文提出SHIFT框架，通过轻量级门控模块（仅训练0.01%参数）自适应调节LLM内部表征，解决检索增强生成中上下文知识与参数化知识的冲突问题，在六个数据集上验证了有效性。

  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: RAG系统中检索到的上下文与LLM参数化知识常存在冲突，现有方法通过编辑神经元缓解冲突，但会导致级联效应损害模型通用能力。

Method: 提出SHIFT框架，将神经元级修改重新表述为可学习门控调制，为LLM附加轻量级门控模块（冻结骨干模型），仅优化少于0.01%的可训练参数，在生成时自适应调节内部表征以平衡上下文与参数化知识。

Result: 在六个数据集上的实验表明SHIFT优于多种竞争基线方法。

Conclusion: SHIFT通过轻量级门控机制有效解决知识冲突问题，避免了传统神经元编辑的级联副作用，代码与数据集已开源。

Abstract: Retrieval-augmented generation (RAG) enhances LLMs by incorporating external knowledge to support response generation. However, conflicts between retrieved context and parametric knowledge have emerged as a critical challenge in RAG systems. To mitigate such conflicts, numerous studies have attempted to identify and edit knowledge-related internal neurons, aiming to improve the ability of LLMs to rely on contextual evidence during generation. However, these neuron-level approaches may introduce unintended cascading effects that compromise the general capabilities of LLMs, as the modified neurons are often entangled with broader model behaviors and functionalities. In this paper, we introduce SHIFT, a novel framework that reformulates neuron-level modification as learnable gate modulation, allowing LLMs to adaptively regulate internal activations for knowledge conflict resolution. Technically, our SHIFT equips LLMs with a lightweight gate module and optimizes fewer than 0.01% trainable parameters while keeping the backbone model frozen. During generation, the gate module adjusts the model's internal representations to adaptively leverage contextual and parametric knowledge. Extensive experiments on six datasets validate the effectiveness of our SHIFT in comparison with various competing baselines. All datasets and code are available at https://github.com/OpenBMB/SHIFT.

### [25] [NLL-Guided Full-Attention Layer Selection for Training-Free Sliding-Window Adaptation](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.27791)
*Qiong Tang,Xiangkun Hu,Xiangyang Liu,Yiran Chen,Yunfan Shao*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: 提出了一种无需训练的NLL引导层选择方法，通过计算每层使用滑动窗口注意力替代全注意力的负对数似然退化程度来衡量层重要性，在仅用1/4全注意力层的情况下达到与1/2全注意力层基线相当的准确率，显著提升了长上下文推理的效率-精度帕累托前沿。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 混合注意力模型中哪些层应保留全注意力是一个未解决的关键问题，现有方法使用固定周期模式或基于注意力的启发式方法，可能无法捕捉对下游精度真正重要的因素。

Method: 提出NLL引导的层选择方法，这是一种无需训练的方法，通过计算每层使用滑动窗口注意力替代全注意力时在答案token上的负对数似然退化程度，直接衡量每层的重要性。

Result: 在LongMemEval上用Qwen3-4B，仅用1/4全注意力层达到64.6%准确率，匹配1/2全注意力层的周期基线(65.0%)，计算预算减半；比SWAA报告的周期1/4全注意力基线高10.4个百分点，比LightTransfer风格基线高26.4个百分点。

Conclusion: 去混杂分析表明该信号与长距离注意力需求一致，而非通用的层敏感性。该方法仅需约15分钟的一次性校准，推进了长上下文LLM部署的效率-精度帕累托前沿。

Abstract: Hybrid attention models that mix full and sliding-window attention across layers offer a promising approach to efficient long-context inference, but the critical question of \emph{which layers} should retain full attention remains unsolved. Existing methods use either fixed periodic patterns or attention-based heuristics that may not capture what matters for downstream accuracy. We propose NLL-guided layer selection, a training-free method that directly measures each layer's importance by computing the negative log-likelihood degradation on answer tokens when that layer uses sliding-window instead of full attention. On LongMemEval with Qwen3-4B, our method achieves 64.6\% accuracy using only 1/4 full-attention layers, matching the 1/2-FA periodic baseline (65.0\%) while halving the computational budget. NLL-guided selection outperforms the SWAA-reported periodic 1/4-FA baseline by 10.4 percentage points and a matched LightTransfer-style baseline by 26.4 percentage points. De-confounding analysis shows the signal is consistent with long-range attention needs rather than generic layer sensitivity. The method requires only $\sim$15 minutes of one-time calibration, advancing the efficiency-accuracy Pareto frontier for long-context LLM deployment.

</details>


### [26] [Position Bias Correction is Insufficient for One-Pass Attention Sorting](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.27793)
*Qiong Tang,Xiangkun Hu,Xiangyang Liu,Yiran Chen,Yunfan Shao*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: 本文提出Debiased One-Pass Attention Sorting，通过估计位置偏差曲线来纠正注意力分数，实现单次排序，但实验表明该方法无法完全替代迭代排序的效果。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 长上下文语言模型存在位置偏差（position bias），中间位置信息未被充分利用。现有Attention Sorting方法通过迭代重排序文档来解决，但多次排序-生成循环导致部署成本过高。作者希望用单次排序替代多次迭代，降低计算开销。

Method: 从低注意力分值的多数文档中估计每个提示的位置偏差曲线，然后通过减法或除法来校正原始注意力分数，实现单次排序（One-Pass Sorting）。

Result: 在LLaMA-2-7B-32K-Instruct上，去偏方法结果与未校准单次排序相同（94.83%包含准确率）；在YaRN-Llama-2-7b-64k上，去偏方法提升8.67个百分点，但仍比迭代排序低14.84个百分点，仅缩小了37%的差距。

Conclusion: 位置偏差校正不足以匹配迭代排序的性能，重复重排序（repeated reordering）带来的额外收益超出了单纯的偏差校正。

Abstract: Long-context language models suffer from position bias, where information in middle positions is underutilized. Attention Sorting addresses this by iteratively reordering documents based on attention patterns, but its multiple sort-and-generate cycles increase deployment cost. We hypothesize that position bias is the primary bottleneck and propose Debiased One-Pass Attention Sorting, which estimates a per-prompt position-bias curve from the low-attention majority of documents and uses it to correct raw attention scores (via subtraction or division) to enable single-pass sorting. Our experiments on two models refute this hypothesis in the tested setting: on LLaMA-2-7B-32K-Instruct, debiasing produces identical results to uncalibrated single-pass sorting (94.83\% containment accuracy), while on YaRN-Llama-2-7b-64k, debiasing improves accuracy by 8.67 percentage points but remains 14.84pp behind iterative sorting, closing only 37\% of the gap. These results suggest that position-bias correction is insufficient to match iterative sorting, and that repeated reordering provides additional benefits beyond bias correction.

### [27] [Learning Complementary Action Modeling from Automotive Maintenance Instructions](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.27808)

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 汽车维修说明中，微小词汇变化（如动作短语的改变）会彻底反转指令的程序性含义，而句子其余部分保持不变。现有方法无法捕捉这种细微但关键的语义差异。

Method: 定义CAM任务，采用候选匹配和受控Seq2Seq生成方法，在德语汽车维修数据集上，通过检索评估、重叠评估和人工评估三个维度进行测试。

Result: 互补性维修指令应建模为基于微妙词汇线索的程序性关联，不能简单视为句子相似性或同义词改写问题。

Conclusion: CAM任务证明了动作短语在决定程序性关系中的核心作用，揭示了传统句子相似度模型在此类任务中的局限性。

Abstract: A minute lexical variation can reverse the procedural meaning of an instruction even when the rest of the sentence remains unchanged. In automotive maintenance instructions, this pattern often appears when an action phrase turns an instruction into its procedural counterpart. The entities, modifiers, and surrounding context remain largely invariant, while the action phrase determines the procedural relation. We define this task as Complementary Action Modeling (CAM). Given a maintenance instruction, the goal is to identify or generate its procedural counterpart by modifying the action phrase while preserving the remaining sentence context. This task focuses on three aspects: distinguishing complementarity from surface similarity, controlling generation at the action-phrase level, and evaluating relational correctness using retrieval, overlap-based, and human evaluation. Using a German automotive maintenance dataset, we examine these questions through candidate matching and controlled Seq2Seq generation. The results show that complementary maintenance instructions are best modeled as procedural associations grounded in subtle lexical cues. They should therefore not be treated as ordinary cases of sentence similarity or synonym-based paraphrasing.

### [29] [Triadic Werewolf: A Jester Role for Multi-Hop Theory of Mind in LLMs](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.27909)
*Avni Mittal*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: 本文通过引入"小丑"（Jester）第三方阵营扩展了狼人杀游戏，发现LLM在三方博弈中存在严重的推理缺陷：GPT-4.1狼人会做出投票淘汰小丑的自毁行为，小丑胜率高达60-70%，仅DeepSeek学会"看似可疑但不故意可疑"的微妙策略。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 传统LLM心智理论评估使用二元社交推理游戏，每个可观察线索都指向一个隐藏身份，模型仅凭强大的语言先验就能取得好成绩，而无需真正模拟对手的动机。作者引入三方利益结构（小丑的获胜条件与同伴怀疑呈反比），以暴露二元博弈无法检测的推理缺陷。

Method: 将狼人杀游戏扩展为三方阵营（村民、狼人、小丑），其中小丑通过被投票出局获胜。在GPT-4.1、DeepSeek-V3.1、Llama-3.3-70B上进行了60场游戏，设置了小丑自学习开启和关闭两种条件。

Result: 小丑胜率60-70%，狼人从未超过20%；GPT-4.1狼人在60-70%的游戏中首日投票淘汰小丑（严格自毁行为）；自学习帮助DeepSeek和Llama但损害GPT-4.1，且代价落在村民而非狼人身上；仅DeepSeek学会"看似可疑但不故意可疑"的微妙策略。

Conclusion: 三方激励结构暴露了二元推演游戏无法发现的、更深层次的多智能体推理缺陷。当前LLM在需要同时推理三个对立效用函数的场景中表现糟糕，尤其是GPT-4.1存在系统性的自毁投票行为。

Abstract: Theory-of-mind evaluations of large language models typically use dyadic social-deduction games, where every observable cue points to a single hidden side, so a model with strong language priors can score well without ever simulating opponents' incentives. We extend the Werewolf game with a Jester, a third faction whose utility on peer suspicion is inverted because it wins by being voted out, so optimal play requires reasoning across three opposing utility functions. Across 60 games on GPT-4.1, DeepSeek-V3.1, and Llama-3.3-70B with Jester self-learning on and off, the Jester wins 60-70% of games while Werewolves never exceed 20%, and GPT-4.1 wolves vote the Jester out on day 1 in 60-70% of games, a strictly self-defeating action. Self-learning helps DeepSeek and Llama but hurts GPT-4.1, with the cost landing on Villagers rather than Werewolves. Only DeepSeek learns the subtle strategy of looking suspicious without looking intentionally suspicious, and it gains the most from the loop. Triadic incentive structure exposes a layer of multi-agent reasoning that dyadic deduction games leave invisible.

### [30] [VASAE: Naming SAE Dictionary Directions with Vocabulary-Aligned Anchoring](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.27941)
*Kairui Zhang,Ziwen Yu,Zahraa S. Abdallah,Martha Lewis*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: 本文提出词汇对齐稀疏自编码器（VASAE），通过在训练中引入词汇对齐锚定，使每个学到的特征与最接近的token嵌入相关联，从而为SAE特征赋予内在的token名称，在不降低重建质量的前提下实现特征与词汇的对齐。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 标准SAE学到的特征通常是事后命名（post hoc），缺乏与Transformer token词汇表的直接连接，导致特征的可解释性受限。

Method: 提出VASAE方法，在训练SAE时引入词汇对齐锚定，将每个特征与最接近的token字符串（即其嵌入最近的token）绑定为内在名称。

Result: 在GPT-2-small上，层0-10约90%特征对齐；在Llama-3.1-8B中，浅层和中层字典分别有92.8%的特征强对齐，但最后一层对齐有限；减去句子级平均稀疏编码后，许多内在token名称与邻近输入token相关。

Conclusion: 词汇对齐锚定能够在训练过程中将学到的特征与内在token名称连接起来，补充事后解读学习字典的方法。

Abstract: Sparse autoencoders (SAEs) provide useful decompositions of Transformer residual streams, but their learned features are usually named post hoc rather than directly connected to the Transformer's token vocabulary. We introduce Vocabulary-Aligned Sparse Autoencoder (VASAE), a method that trains SAE features under vocabulary-aligned anchoring and assigns each feature an intrinsic token name: the token string whose embedding is nearest to that feature. Without reducing reconstruction quality compared with a standard SAE, VASAE produces dictionaries with vocabulary-aligned features. Using a 0.8 cutoff on the nearest-token alignment score, dictionaries trained on GPT-2-small post-residual streams align about 90% of features in layers 0--10. In Llama-3.1-8B, representative shallow and middle-layer dictionaries contain strongly aligned features, including 92.8% in the shallow layer, while the representative final-layer dictionary shows limited alignment. After subtracting the sentence-level mean sparse code, case studies show that many remaining intrinsic token names are relevant to nearby input tokens. These results suggest that vocabulary-aligned anchoring can connect learned features to intrinsic token names during training, complementing post hoc interpretation of learned dictionaries.

As a result, the detection of factual errors in human-written text has been relatively neglected. To address this gap, we first distill a taxonomy of human-induced factual errors by analyzing corrections of newspaper articles, a representative source of text that is guaranteed to be human-written and contains few grammatical errors. Our analysis revealed that there are characteristic categories such as kanji misconversions and numeral classifier errors, which are not focused in existing hallucination benchmarks. Based on the taxonomy, we then evaluate the FED capability of vanilla LLMs on synthesized realistic test cases and real corrections. *Chengxiao Dai,Zhaokun Yan,Zhanhui Lin*

TL;DR: 本文提出信号-覆盖率矩阵，将LLM自动形式化的输出按Lean编译器通过/失败与语义等价/不等价分为四类，发现TC%提升主要来自类型层级恢复（约64%），语义修复净效果为零，呼吁用细粒度指标而非单一标量衡量进展。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 当前LLM自动形式化的TC%从53%提升到76%，但单一标量无法揭示具体解决了哪些错误。需要细粒度分析框架区分类型错误和语义错误的修复情况。

Method: 提出信号-覆盖率矩阵，交叉Lean编译器结果（通过/失败）与语义等价性判断（等价/不等价），将输出分为真成功(TS)、仅类型(TO)、仅语义(SO)、双失败(BF)四类。在ProofNet#和MiniF2F-test上用DeepSeek V4-Pro测试了Vanilla、Lean-Retry、Sample-Filter、SAF四种方法。

Result: (1) TS提升+34~+36，其中~64%来自类型层级恢复，SO净变化为零（87.5%语义错误被修复，但新产生8个）。(2) TO→TS转化率为23/61（95%CI 26.6%-50.3%），该转化率可预测其他方法的ΔTS误差在2/186以内，且使ΔTC与Vanilla编译失败率呈线性关系（R²=0.96）。(3) 两个判断器在elab-feedback输出上分歧26-37pp（Vanilla仅7pp），30-56%的符号判断器假阴性可追溯到编译器强制改写。残差最终归因于两个金标准形式化错误。

Conclusion: TC%提升应归因于哪个单元格发生了变化，而非仅看标量数值。建议采用细粒度矩阵报告自动形式化进展。

Abstract: Headline type-correctness (TC\%) of LLM autoformalization has climbed from $\sim$53\% to $\sim$76\% in two years, yet this scalar conceals which errors each method resolves. We propose a signal-coverage matrix that crosses the Lean elaborator (pass/fail) with a semantic-equivalence judgment (equivalent/not), sorting every output into one of four cells: true success (TS), type-only (TO), semantic-only (SO), or both fail (BF). On ProofNet\# and MiniF2F-test with DeepSeek V4-Pro across Vanilla, Lean-Retry, Sample-Filter, and Stratified Autoformalization (SAF): (1) the +34 to +36 TS gain across the three elab-feedback methods is $\sim$64\% type-stratum recovery, with SO flat on net (87.5\% of original semantic errors rescued, 8 newly created). (2) The TO-to-TS rate is 23/61 for each method (Wilson 95\% CI [26.6\%, 50.3\%]), and this stratum-level recovery rate predicts $Δ$TS on held-out methods to within 2/186 and renders $Δ$TC linear in the Vanilla elab-fail rate across six (model, dataset) cells ($R^2=0.96$). (3) The two judges disagree by 26 to 37 pp on elab-feedback outputs (vs. 7 pp on Vanilla), with 30 to 56\% of symbolic-judge false negatives traceable to elaborator-forced rewrites. The persistent residual reduces to two gold-formalization errors. TC\% gains should be credited by which cell moved, not by the scalar alone.

</details>

### [37] [Can LLMs Judge Better Than They Generate? Evaluating Task Asymmetry, Mechanistic Interpretability and Transferability for In-Context QA](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.28050)
*Sambaran Bandyopadhyay*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: 本文通过受控上下文QA实验发现，自我评估并非天生比生成更容易，生成准确率在4个基准中的3个上高于自我评估，且注意力分析显示评估对上下文的关注度远低于生成，挑战了LLM自我评估管线的基本假设。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 检验LLM-as-a-Judge和自我评估管线中"评估比生成更容易"这一隐含假设是否正确。

Method: 在受控的上下文QA场景中（将上下文段落作为唯一信息源），让模型对自己生成的答案进行评判，排除开放域比较中的参数知识混淆。使用4个基准（SQuAD 2.0, DROP, HotpotQA, MuSiQue）和2个模型进行实验，并结合注意力分析和LoRA微调验证。

Result: 1) 评估并非普遍比生成更容易：生成准确率在3/4基准上高于自我评估，仅多跳MuSiQue例外；2) 注意力分析发现评估对上下文的关注度比生成低3-5倍，且几乎不阅读候选答案；3) LoRA微调证实不对称性非训练伪影：生成微调导致过度接受，评估微调导致生成能力退化。

Conclusion: 自我评估管线中的核心假设存在问题，评估并不总是比生成更简单。

Abstract: LLM-as-a-Judge and self-evaluation pipelines implicitly assume that evaluation is easier than generation. We test this in a controlled in-context QA setting where a context passage is the sole information source and each model judges the answer it generated, removing the parametric-knowledge confound of open-domain comparisons. Across four benchmarks (SQuAD 2.0, DROP, HotpotQA, MuSiQue) and two models, evaluation is not uniformly easier: generation accuracy exceeds self-evaluation on three of four, with multi-hop MuSiQue the exception. Attention analysis reveals why: evaluation attends to context 3--5x less than generation does and barely reads the candidate answer. LoRA fine-tuning confirms the asymmetry is not a training artifact: generation fine-tuning induces over-acceptance and evaluation fine-tuning degrades generation. These findings challenge core assumptions in self-evaluation pipelines.

</details>


### [38] [MultiHashFormer: Hash-based Generative Language Models](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.28057)
*Huiyin Xue,Atsuki Yamaguchi,Nikolaos Aletras*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: MultiHashFormer通过哈希签名替代传统嵌入矩阵，实现参数量恒定的因果语言模型，在100M到3B参数规模上超越标准Transformer。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 传统语言模型的嵌入矩阵随词表大小线性增长，参数开销大。已有哈希方法存在多对一碰撞问题，无法用于因果语言模型。

Method: 每个token由多个独立哈希函数生成唯一哈希签名（短哈希ID序列），通过Hash Encoder压缩为潜在向量供Transformer解码器处理，再由Hash Decoder生成下一token的哈希签名并映射回文本。

Result: 在100M、1B、3B参数规模上，MultiHashFormer在多个基准测试中一致优于标准Transformer LM，且支持多语言词表扩展而参数不变。

Conclusion: 基于哈希签名的方案有效解决了嵌入矩阵参数膨胀问题，同时避免了哈希碰撞对自回归建模的干扰，实现了参数高效且性能更优的语言模型。

Abstract: Language models (LMs) represent tokens using embedding matrices that scale linearly with the vocabulary size. To constrain the parameter footprint, prior work proposes hashing many tokens into a single vector within encoder-only models. While this offers parameter efficiency, many-to-one collisions prevent its use in causal LMs. In this paper, we propose MultiHashFormer, a new framework that allows hash-based autoregression. Each token is represented as a unique hash signature, a short sequence of discrete hash IDs, generated by multiple independent hash functions. A Hash Encoder compresses this signature into a single latent vector for processing by a Transformer decoder. Then, a Hash Decoder generates the hash signature of the next token, which is then mapped back to text. We evaluate our approach at the 100M, 1B and 3B parameter scales, demonstrating that MultiHashFormer consistently outperforms standard Transformer LMs across multiple benchmarks. Furthermore, we show that our model handles multilingual vocabulary expansion with a constant parameter footprint without any modifications.

</details>


### [39] [Mechanism-Driven Monitors for Preemptive Detection of LLM Training Instability](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.28116)
*Ruixuan Huang,Yipei Wang,Wenyi Fang,Hantao Huang,Yifan Huang,Ansheng You,Zhenxing Zhang,Shuai Wang,Fan Wu,Yang Zheng*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: 针对大语言模型训练中的稳定性故障，本文提出从关键模块的功能角色出发推导内部监控信号，在低精度Flash Attention和MoE路由器中分别利用谱熵和专家选择指标，实现对数值故障和超参数故障的早期检测，比损失发散提前数千步发出预警。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 大语言模型训练耗时长、计算量大，训练稳定性故障一旦发生，可能在损失和梯度范数看似正常的情况下持续数千步而不被发现，造成巨大资源浪费。现有检测手段往往等到损失发散才能察觉故障，缺乏更早期的预警机制。

Method: 提出机制驱动的训练不稳定检测方法：(1) 针对低精度Flash Attention，监控QK双线性分解的谱熵，其一阶项在损失完全崩溃前就会出现异常；(2) 针对MoE路由器，从专家选择的功能角色推导指示指标；(3) 通过故障注入实验验证方法有效性，涵盖低精度注意力、大学习率及组合故障。

Result: 在低精度注意力、大学习率和组合故障的故障注入实验中，所提出的信号能为不同故障提供独特的特征标识，在损失发散前数千步即可触发预警。

Conclusion: 机制驱动的内部监控信号能够比现有方法更早地检测到训练稳定性故障，为大规模LLM训练的稳定性保障提供了新的技术路径。

Abstract: Frontier large language model training consumes massive accelerator fleets and long wall-clock computation, making stability failures costly when they occur. After a numerical or a hyperparameter fault has already destabilized the training dynamics, it may continue for thousands of steps while loss and gradient norms still appear normal. We study mechanism-driven detection of training instability by deriving internal monitors from the functional role of each critical module and from the earliest computational sites where failures are expected to produce measurable signatures. For low-precision flash attention, we monitor the spectral entropy of a QK bilinear decomposition, whose first-order term becomes abnormal before the loss fully collapses. For MoE routers, we derive indicators from their role in expert selection. Our fault-injection experiments on low-precision attention, large learning-rate, and combined faults show that these signals provide distinct signatures for different failures, triggering thousands of steps before loss divergence.

### [40] [From Tokens to States: LLMs as a Special Case of World Models and the Continuous Path Beyond](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.28127)
*Paul Dubois*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: 本文主张LLMs是世界模型的一个退化特例，而非替代品；并提出从NTP到JEPA存在连续光谱，同时指出沿着这个光谱前进会牺牲LLM的两大可扩展性优势（互联网规模自监督数据和适配离散预测的Transformer架构），这两者仍是开放问题。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 当前AI社区将LLMs与世界模型对立起来（LeCun认为应放弃自回归token预测转向潜在空间架构），这种二元框架过于简化，阻碍了对两者关系的正确理解。

Method: 提出两个核心论点：(1) LLMs是世界模型的退化特例——状态空间为所有token序列，唯一动作是追加一个token；(2) 从NTP到JEPA存在连续光谱，中间包括多token预测、未来摘要预测、下一潜在预测等现有工作。

Result: 揭示了沿着光谱前进会逐渐失去LLM的两个实际优势：自监督文本数据的可扩展性，以及为离散token预测协同设计的Transformer架构。

Conclusion: 提出了两个开放问题：(1) 数据问题——从自监督文本到带标注动作的环境之间存在悬崖；(2) 架构问题——Transformer能否泛化到连续状态预测，还是需要新的基础算子。

Abstract: The AI community has framed the relationship between large language models (LLMs) and world models as a dichotomy: LLMs predict tokens; world models simulate reality. Yann LeCun argues in 2022 that reaching general intelligence requires abandoning autoregressive token prediction in favour of latent-space architectures. This framing is unnecessarily binary. Two claims will be defended. First, LLMs are a degenerate special case of world models: the state space is the set of all token sequences, the only action is appending one token, and world models are therefore a strict generalisation of LLMs, not a replacement. Second, there is a natural continuous spectrum from NTP to JEPA, with multi-token prediction, future-summary prediction, and next-latent prediction as intermediate stations already populated by current research. Moving along this spectrum relaxes the LLM constraints one by one. It also progressively surrenders the two practical advantages that make LLMs trainable at scale: internet-scale self-supervised data, and a transformer architecture co-designed for discrete token prediction. Both are examined as open research questions: the data question (the cliff from self-supervised text to instrumented action-labelled environments) and the architecture question (whether the transformer generalises to continuous-state prediction, or whether a new primitive is needed).

### [41] [Vision-Default, Prior-Override: Causal Mechanisms of Perception-Knowledge Conflict in Vision-Language Models](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.28273)
*Niclas Lietzow,Danielle Bitterman,Carsten Eickhoff,William Rudman,Michal Golovanevsky*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: 本文通过激活修补、消融研究和机制分析，发现视觉-语言模型中视觉信息默认主导，而先验知识仅依赖一小部分注意力头（2.5-4.8%），这些头集中在网络后半部分，构成稀疏因果回路，不对称地调控视觉与知识冲突。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有研究仅从行为层面描述VLM如何处理视觉与先验知识的冲突，缺乏组件级别的因果解释，因此需要从机制层面揭示其内部处理逻辑。

Method: 采用三种粒度的激活修补（残差流、注意力头、MLP子层），结合模型组件消融实验和机制分析，在三个VLM家族上进行系统研究。

Result: 视觉默认主导；先验知识依赖一小部分注意力头（2.5-4.8%，集中在网络后半部分）；消融这些头使68-96%的先验知识预测转为视觉预测，但仅改变0.8-7.5%的视觉预测；这些头分为路由头和写入头，结构跨模型和规模一致。

Conclusion: 揭示了一个稀疏的因果回路机制，解释了VLM如何在感知与先验知识冲突时进行决策，且该机制具有跨模型家族和规模的一致性和不对称性。

Abstract: Vision-language models must reconcile visual evidence with memorized world knowledge when the two conflict. How they resolve this conflict shapes the reliability of multimodal systems, yet prior work characterizes it behaviorally without a component-level causal account. We combine activation patching across three granularities (residual stream, attention heads, and MLP sublayers) with model-component ablation studies and mechanistic analysis. Across three VLM families, we find that visual grounding emerges by default, whereas prior grounding depends on a small set of causally necessary attention heads (2.5-4.8%) concentrated in the second half of the network. These heads enable answers from stored world knowledge (e.g., "red" for a strawberry) despite conflicting visual input. Ablating them flips predictions from knowledge-grounded to visually grounded answers in 68-96% of cases under prior-knowledge prompts, but changes only 0.8-7.5% of visually grounded predictions, establishing an asymmetric causal structure. The identified heads decompose into routing heads, which modulate information flow, and writing heads, which directly project answer tokens into the residual stream. This structure is consistent across model families and scales, revealing a sparse causal circuit underlying perception-knowledge conflict in VLMs.

  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 构建多周期MILP模型，联合优化机队采购（传统/电动飞机）、充电基础设施部署、航线服务分配，并纳入排放目标、电动服务份额和预算等政策约束。

Conclusion: 电动航空转型需要机队规模、航班调度和航线优先级三方面的协调规划，而非单纯依赖充电设施建设。

Abstract: This paper presents a multi-period mixed-integer linear programming (MILP) framework for planning the transition from conventional to electric aircraft in regional aviation. The model jointly optimizes fleet acquisition, infrastructure deployment, and service allocation over time, while accounting for policy constraints such as emissions reduction targets, electric service share, and budget limits. A real-world case study based on Helijet's short-haul network in British Columbia demonstrates the applicability of the model. The results show that electrification can reduce emissions by more than 70\% within five years while remaining economically viable. However, the transition is primarily limited by the capacity of the fleet and operational structure, rather than the charging infrastructure, leading to unmet demand under direct aircraft replacement. These findings emphasize the need for coordinated planning across fleet sizing, scheduling, and route prioritization to ensure a practical and efficient transition to electric aviation.

### [43] [OverFlowLight: Real-Time Gridlock Prevention and Traffic Signal Optimization for Urban Intersections](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.27381)
*Mingyuan Li,Boyang Huang,Tianqi Jiang,Chenpu Li,Chunyu Liu,Yang Li,Ruimin Li,Qiang Wu*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: OverFlowLight是一个结合摄像头与雷达多模态感知、混合规则与强化学习控制的实时交通信号控制框架，能在检测到排队溢出时动态插入专用相位清除阻塞队列。在三个城市43个路口的真实部署中，减少60.4%的溢出现象，提升18.2%的网络吞吐量。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有交通信号控制算法主要优化通行效率，但在高峰时段无法有效应对排队溢出问题，导致级联拥堵和安全风险。

Method: 1) 利用摄像头和雷达多模态感知实时检测溢出；2) 动态生成并插入专用溢出相位清除阻塞队列；3) 混合控制：规则驱动的快速溢出干预 + 强化学习等后端控制器实现长程效率优化。

Result: 在三城市43个路口真实部署，溢出现象减少60.4%，网络吞吐量提升18.2%，显著减少手动干预需求。

Conclusion: 首个实用、可扩展、数据驱动的主动防堵框架，是构建韧性高效城市交通系统的关键组件。

Abstract: Queue overflow, a severe consequence of urban traffic congestion, occurs when vehicle queues exceed intersection capacity, obstructing upstream traffic and triggering cascading gridlocks. Prevailing traffic signal control (TSC) algorithms, primarily optimized for throughput, often fail to address overflow during peak hours, exacerbating congestion and creating safety hazards. We propose OverFlowLight, a real-time framework designed to preemptively resolve overflow and enhance overall TSC performance. It first introduces a mechanism to accurately detect overflow in real-time by leveraging multi-modal sensing from cameras and radars. Upon detection, it dynamically generates and inserts dedicated overflow phases into the signal cycle to clear the blocking queues. This is orchestrated by a hybrid control design that combines rapid rule-based overflow intervention with controller back ends such as reinforcement learning (RL) for longer-horizon efficiency. We conducted extensive real-world deployments of OverFlowLight across 43 intersections in three major cities. The framework demonstrates seamless integration with existing RL-based TSC agents, highlighting its modularity and practical applicability. Empirical results show that OverFlowLight reduces overflow incidents by 60.4% and increases network throughput by 18.2% compared to deployed baselines. Furthermore, it substantially diminishes the need for manual intervention common with expert-tuned signal plans. This work presents the first practical, scalable, and data-driven framework for actively preventing traffic gridlock, offering a crucial component for building resilient and efficient urban transportation systems. Our demonstration videos, codes and datasets are available at the anonymous URL, https://anonymous.4open.science/r/OverFlowLight-FBF9.

### [44] [RANSAC Scoring Done Right](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.27385)
*James Pritts,Felix Seegräber,Kevin Köser*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种新的RANSAC评分函数，通过对内点尺度进行解析边际化（而非估计），消除了对用户提供的尺度参数的依赖，在近7万对图像基准上达到了超越现有方法的效果。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有RANSAC变体依赖用户提供的内点尺度参数来评分，但该参数需从受污染数据中估计，这导致算法对阈值敏感且需要人工调参。

Method: 逆转常规推理顺序：不对内点尺度进行估计，而是在共轭逆伽马先验下对内点尺度进行解析闭式边际化，然后优化数据分区。该闭式表达式统一了无信息Jeffreys极限和有信息经验贝叶斯先验，通过排序扫描实现O(N log N)计算。

Result: 在近7万对图像基准上，该方法在阈值误校准下保持稳定（基线方法性能下降），仅需2个验证对即可达到近最优精度（基线需要约100倍更多数据），且在验证数据稀缺时收紧先验正则化。

Conclusion: 提出的评分是首个真正消除了内点尺度参数的RANSAC评分函数，在不同数据丰裕度下自适应，无需改变算法，达到了超越现有方法的性能。

Abstract: The most widely used RANSAC variants score candidate models by counting inliers or summing per-point scores that saturate beyond a residual threshold. Every such score requires a user-supplied parameter that is a function of the inlier scale, which must itself be estimated from contaminated data. We remove this dependence by reversing the usual order of inference: rather than estimating the scale and then scoring against it, we marginalize the inlier scale analytically in closed form under a conjugate Inverse-Gamma prior for a fixed inlier partition, then optimize over partitions. A single closed-form expression spans the non-informative Jeffreys limit and informative empirical-Bayes priors, so the same score adapts across data-rich and data-scarce regimes without any change to the algorithm. The proposed RANSAC score is the first in which the inlier scale is genuinely absent from the formula. The score admits O(N log N ) computation via sort-and-sweep. On a benchmark of nearly 70 000 image pairs spanning different two-view estimation problems and both engineered and learned feature pipelines, the proposed score exceeds the state of the art (RANSAC, MSAC, GaU, MAGSAC): it stays nearly flat under threshold miscalibration where baselines degrade, reaches near-optimal accuracy from as few as two validation pairs where baselines need ont he order of 100 times more,. and tightens its prior regularization as validation data grows scarce.

</details>

### [48] [Learning in Markovian bandits with non-observable states and constrained decision epochs](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.27448)
*Thomas Hira,Victor Boone,Urtzi Ayesta,Ina Maria Verloop*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本文研究马尔可夫强盗中状态不可观测且决策时刻可能受限的遗憾最小化问题，提出自退化马尔可夫强盗模型，设计了UCB-NOM算法，证明无先验知识时遗憾超对数增长，但有先验知识时可达到对数遗憾。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 传统马尔可夫强盗假设状态可观测，但实际中状态往往不可观测或观测成本高。同时，许多场景存在决策时刻受限的情况，如推荐系统中不能频繁切换推荐策略。作者希望在这种更具挑战性的设定下，探索能否实现低遗憾的学习。

Method: 首先提出自退化马尔可夫强盗（self-degrading Markovian bandits）模型，证明纯策略在此类问题中渐近最优。然后设计UCB-NOM算法，基于乐观原则处理状态不可观测性。算法在无先验知识时实现近对数遗憾，在给定偏置函数上界先验知识时达到严格对数遗憾。

Result: 1）无先验知识时，少切换臂的算法必然产生超对数遗憾（ω(log T)）。2）UCB-NOM在无先验知识时实现近对数遗憾。3）有偏置函数上界先验知识时，UCB-NOM达到O(log T)遗憾，且最坏情况遗憾界为O(√(T log T))。4）所有遗憾界不依赖于马尔可夫链的状态数。

Conclusion: 状态不可观测性在自退化马尔可夫强盗中只是"轻微不便"，通过合理算法设计（如UCB-NOM）仍能获得近乎最优的遗憾性能。少切换的要求确实带来根本性困难，但先验知识可有效弥补。

Abstract: This paper studies the problem of regret minimization in Markovian bandits with \emph{non-observable states} and possibly \emph{constrained} decision epochs. The focus is restricted to a ``pure'' regret benchmark, that compares the performance of the learning algorithm to the best \emph{pure policy} which -- akin to optimal policies of stochastic bandits -- picks the optimal arm from start to finish without ever switching. We introduce a generalization of rested Markovian bandits, \emph{self-degrading Markovian bandits}, for which pure policies are always asymptotically optimal.We show that without prior knowledge on the underlying bandit, the regret of algorithms that switch arms rarely necessarily scales super-logarithmically for every bandit, i.e., as $ω(\log(T))$, where $T$ is the learning horizon. Despite the unreachability of the logarithmic regime, we design UCB-NOM, an optimistic algorithm inspired by UCB, of which the regret is nearly logarithmic. Lastly, we show that given prior knowledge on the Markovian bandit in the form of a bound on the bias functions of its arm, a proper instantiation of UCB-NOM achieves $O(\log(T))$ regret. We further show that this prior knowledge allows for a $O(\sqrt{T \log(T)})$ worst-case regret bound for UCB-NOM. Notably, our regret bounds do not depend on the number of states of the underlying Markov chains. Our findings suggest that the non-observability of states is a mild inconvenience in self-degrading Markovian bandits.

Abstract: Benchmarks of machine learning models often include many datasets, making evaluation expensive.   We introduce a framework to perform the task of selecting datasets subsets with an evaluation of how different selection strategies preserve the global model rankings. Our framework includes bootstrap aggregation, which provides valid confidence intervals, allowing a principled comparison of selection strategies. We consider clustering, design criteria (A/D-optimality), random baselines, and greedy farthest-first (FAFI). For the latter, we derive upper bounds on selection quality in terms of ranking errors as a function of the number of selected datasets.

*Shubham Aggarwal*

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Abstract: Multi-head attention conventionally partitions the hidden dimension equally across all heads at every layer, enforcing an identical representational subspace dimension (dh = dmodel/h) throughout the models depth. In this work, we identify this uniform allocation as a fundamental structural bottleneck: due to their restricted dimensional space, early-layer heads are unable to faithfully capture complex, high-dimensional contextual patterns. To resolve this, we introduce the Prism Transformer, a novel architectural paradigm that replaces the static, uniform head configuration with a progressive head schedule. By monotonically increasing the head count across layers, the Prism Transformer naturally establishes a local-to-global representational hierarchy: early layers leverage fewer, exceptionally wide heads to capture complex, local compositional patterns, while deep layers deploy many, narrow heads to decompose these patterns into specialized linguistic features. Crucially, this structural shift is parameter-neutral, compute-neutral, and introduces zero training or inference overhead, preserving identical weight matrices and FLOP budgets as the standard Transformer. Across three model scales (124M, 354M, and 757M), the Prism Transformer consistently outperforms uniform baselines, achieving consistent reductions in validation loss alongside consistent gains on downstream zero-shot benchmarks (including PIQA, HellaSwag, ARC-Easy, and WinoGrande). Our findings demonstrate that non-uniform subspace allocation unlocks latent capacity within the standard Transformer budget, enabling more effective use of model capacity.

### [51] [Dangerous Liaisons of Convex Learning and Non-Affine Aggregation](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.28123)
*Thomas Boudou,Batiste Le Bars,Nirupam Gupta,Aurélien Bellet*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本文证明，在凸学习中，梯度聚合规则保持单调性的充要条件是正仿射变换。非仿射聚合（如自适应、隐私、鲁棒性、公平性约束）会破坏单调性，导致收敛不稳定和泛化性能下降。研究提出了恢复单调性的充分条件，为理解现代学习系统的失效模式提供了统一理论框架。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现代学习系统常采用非仿射梯度聚合规则（如自适应、隐私保护、鲁棒性或公平性约束），但这些规则是否会破坏更新算子的单调性？单调性是保证首次凸优化中最后迭代收敛和泛化性能的关键性质。此前，能否设计保持单调性的非仿射聚合规则是一个未解问题。

Method: 理论证明与必要条件分析：通过严格的数学推导，证明聚合梯度保持单调性的充要条件是聚合规则为正仿射变换。进而量化非仿射聚合对收敛速度和算法稳定性的损害，并识别出恢复单调性的充分条件。

Result: （1）单调性保持的充要条件是正仿射聚合；（2）非仿射聚合必然破坏单调性，导致收敛不稳定和算法稳定性退化；（3）给出了量化分析非仿射聚合负面影响的数学结果；（4）提出了恢复单调性的充分条件。

Conclusion: 非仿射聚合规则（如自适应梯度、隐私噪声、鲁棒聚合等）会不可避免地破坏单调性，从而损害收敛保证和泛化能力。但通过识别适当的充分条件，可以在某些场景下恢复单调性。该工作为解释现代学习系统中不同的失效模式提供了统一的理论框架。

Abstract: Last-iterate convergence and generalization guarantees in first-order convex learning hinge on the monotonicity of the update operator. While linear averaging preserves the monotonicity of gradient updates, this property is often violated when gradients are aggregated non-affinely, as in modern pipelines enforcing constraints like adaptivity, privacy, robustness or fairness. Whether it is possible to design non-affine aggregation rules that maintain monotonicity has remained an open question. We answer this question negatively: we prove that the monotonicity of aggregated gradients is preserved if and only if the aggregation rule is positively affine. Consequently, non-affine aggregation prevents steady convergence and substantially degrade algorithmic stability. We quantify these drawbacks and propose a path forward by identifying sufficient conditions under which monotonicity can be restored. Our results provide a unified theoretical framework explaining the disparate failure modes observed in modern learning systems.

### [52] [Operator Learning for Cubic Nonlinear Schrödinger Equation on Periodic Domains](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.27459)
*Emmanuel E. Oguadimma,Victory C. Obieke,Xueying Yu*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种几何条件化的傅里叶神经算子（FNO），用于二维平环上不同长宽比下的三次非线性薛定谔方程。该算子以解的实部、虚部及长宽比参数ω²为输入，学习单步解算子，能够捕捉有理/无理几何结构下不同的Sobolev范数演化行为。实验表明，显式加入ω²可提升长期预测精度，验证了几何感知神经算子在非线性色散偏微分方程频谱转移现象学习中的有效性。
